Emerging growth company&#160;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" contextRef="duration_2019-12-04_to_2019-12-04" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></span></p> <p style="font-family:Arial;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. <span style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal">&#9744;</span></p> <div style="text-align:center"> <p style="line-height:3pt;border-bottom:0.50px solid #000000;width:100%;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0px">&#160;</p></div> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:0"></p></div> <p style='page-break-before:always'></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" /> <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">Item&#160;5.07. Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders</p> <p style="font-family:Arial;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On December&#160;4, 2019, Microsoft Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) held its 2019 Annual Shareholders Meeting (the &#8220;Annual Meeting&#8221;). There were 7,632,138,696 shares of common stock entitled to be voted at the Annual Meeting, of which 6,610,123,128 were voted in person or by proxy. The results for each item submitted for a vote of shareholders are as follows. The shareholders:</p> <p style="font-family:Arial;margin-left:4%;text-align:left;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">(1) Voted to elect each of the thirteen (13)&#160;nominees for director.</p> <p style="font-family:Arial;margin-left:4%;text-align:left;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">(2) Approved, on an advisory basis, the compensation of the Company&#8217;s named executive officers.</p> <p style="font-family:Arial;margin-left:4%;text-align:left;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">(3) Voted to ratify the appointment of Deloitte&#160;&#038; Touche LLP as the Company&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm for fiscal year 2020.</p> <p style="font-family:Arial;margin-left:4%;text-align:left;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">(4) Rejected a shareholder proposal concerning a report on employee representation on the Board of Directors.</p> <p style="font-family:Arial;margin-left:4%;text-align:left;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">(5) Rejected a shareholder proposal concerning a report on gender pay gap.</p> <p style="font-family:Arial;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Company&#8217;s inspector of election certified the following vote tabulations:</p> <p style="font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Election of Directors</p>
